      "source": [
        "# Create a search box widget\n",
        "search_box = widgets.Text(\n",
        "    value='',\n",
        "    placeholder='Type to search',\n",
        "    description='Search:',\n",
        "    disabled=False\n",
        ")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Create a dropdown widget for the filtered company names\n",
        "dropdown = widgets.SelectMultiple(\n",
        "    options=df['name'].tolist(),\n",
        "    description='Select:',\n",
        "    disabled=False\n",
        ")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Function to filter the company names based on the search query\n",
        "def filter_companies(change):\n",
        "    query = change['new']\n",
        "    filtered_companies = df[df['name'].str.contains(query, case=False, na=False)]['name'].tolist()\n",
        "    dropdown.options = filtered_companies\n",
        "\n",
        "# Attach the filtering function to the search box\n",
        "search_box.observe(filter_companies, names='value')\n",
        "\n",
        "# Display the search box and the dropdown\n",
        "display(search_box, dropdown)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Function to get the selected companies\n",
        "def get_selected_companies(b):\n",
        "    print(\"Selected Companies:\")\n",
        "    for company in dropdown.value:\n",
        "        print(company)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Button to confirm selection\n",
        "select_button = widgets.Button(description=\"Confirm Selection\")\n",
        "select_button.on_click(get_selected_companies)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Display the button\n",
        "display(select_button)\n",
        "\n"
      ]
    },

        "to_compare = [\n",
        "    \"Gross Profit\",\n",
        "    \"Interest Expense\",\n",
        "    \"Assets\",\n",
        "    \"Assets, Current\",\n",

        "to_compare_clean = []\n",

        "        account_name = response.json()\n",

        "df = pd.DataFrame(columns = ['cik']+ variables)\n",
        "\n",
        "for index, row in df_comparables.iterrows():\n",
        "    cik = row['cik']\n",
        "    eps = row['val']\n",
        "    name = row['entityName']\n",
        "    row_new = pd.DataFrame( {var : None for var in variables}, index=[0])\n",
        "    for var in variables:\n",
        "        params = {'cik' : cik, 'tag' : var, 'taxonomy' : 'us-gaap'}\n",
        "        response = requests.get(f\"{BASE_URL}/company_concept\", params=params)\n",
        "        if response.status_code == 200:\n",
        "            reply = response.json()\n",
        "            reply = reply['units']['USD'][-1]['val'] # get the last one\n",
        "            row_new[var] = reply\n",
        "        else:\n",
        "            reply = None\n",
        "            row_new[var] = reply\n",
        "\n",
        "    row_new['cik'] = cik\n",
        "    df = pd.concat([df, row_new], ignore_index=True)\n",
        "\n",
        "df"
      ]
